ARC POSITION: CLIMAX

HOOK_TYPE: decisive action

CLIFFHANGER_TYPE: antagonist's downfall

CHARACTER_FOCUS: Leila

EPISODE 59: The Quiet Aftermath

PREMISE: With Julian imprisoned and his empire dismantled, Leila and Gabriel navigate the immediate aftermath, tending to their wounds and contemplating a future free from constant pursuit, but the world is still adjusting to the fallout.

HOOK: Leila, bandaged but resolute, watches a news report detailing Julian's public disgrace, a faint, almost imperceptible smile playing on her lips.

CORE MOVE: Leila and Gabriel begin to process their shared trauma and envision a life beyond their desperate flight, starting to build a foundation for a new future.

CHARACTER COST: Leila confronts the emptiness left by the destruction of her old life, realizing freedom comes with its own form of loneliness and uncertainty, and the profound shift in her identity.

CLIFFHANGER: Leila receives an unexpected, legitimate offer to lead a new foundation dedicated to corporate ethics, a path that could redefine her purpose, but it requires her to step back into the public eye, a choice she hesitates to make, looking to Gabriel for guidance, a hidden camera lens glinting in the background.

ARC POSITION: RESOLUTION

HOOK_TYPE: reflective peace

CLIFFHANGER_TYPE: new opportunity with hidden threat

CHARACTER_FOCUS: Leila

EPISODE 60: A Lingering Shadow

PREMISE: Leila and Gabriel make a joint decision about their future, choosing to build a life together while acknowledging the lingering shadows of their past, as a cryptic new threat emerges, directly referencing Gabriel's former life.

HOOK: Leila and Gabriel stand on a windswept cliff overlooking the ocean, their hands clasped, a silent agreement passing between them.

CORE MOVE: Leila and Gabriel commit to a shared future, embracing both the peace they've earned and the potential dangers that may follow them.

CHARACTER COST: Gabriel accepts the vulnerability of a stable relationship, letting go of his lone wolf mentality, while Leila embraces a life of constant vigilance, knowing their past will always be a part of their present.

CLIFFHANGER: As Leila and Gabriel watch the sunset, a news alert flashes on Gabriel's burner phone: a shadowy figure, previously thought to be a myth within Julian's network, has resurfaced, leaving a single, untraceable message: "Gabriel Varela. The debt for 'Project Chimera' is long overdue," followed by a distorted image of a familiar locket.

ARC POSITION: RESOLUTION

HOOK_TYPE: romantic commitment

CLIFFHANGER_TYPE: new antagonist revealed

CHARACTER_FOCUS: Gabriel

14

Episode Beats

No content.

15

Season Script — All 60 Episodes

EPISODE 1: THE GOLDEN CAGE

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

A close-up on a delicate hand sketching a charcoal portrait in a small notebook. The hand wears a massive, glittering engagement ring. A man’s hand, wearing an expensive watch, firmly closes the notebook.

SCENE 1 — ART GALLERY GALA - NIGHT

The room buzzes with quiet, wealthy conversation. LEILA ARMAN stands beside her fiancé, JULIAN THORNE. He smiles for a society photographer.

JULIAN

(A perfect smile)

Darling, put that away. Mr. Dubois wants a word about the Zurich acquisition.

LEILA

It’s just a sketch, Julian.

JULIAN

It’s a distraction. Tonight is about business. Our business. Smile.

He places a possessive hand on the small of her back, steering her into the crowd. Leila’s own smile is flawless, practiced, and empty.

SCENE 2 — ALLEY BEHIND GALLERY - CONTINUOUS

Leila slips out a side door, needing a moment of air. The city noise is a distant hum. She leans against the cold brick, closing her eyes.

A shadow detaches from the wall. GABRIEL VARELA.

GABRIEL

Leila Arman.

Leila’s eyes snap open. Before she can scream, his hand clamps over her mouth, a cloth pressed against her face. The smell is sharp, chemical. Her body goes limp. He catches her easily, a ghost lifting a doll.

SCENE 3 — MOVING VAN - LATER

Leila wakes up. The van smells of oil and dust. Her wrists are zip-tied. A strip of black tape covers her mouth.

She sees Gabriel’s eyes in the rearview mirror, cold steel focused on the road. Panic seizes her. She struggles, the plastic cutting into her skin. Her fingers find the familiar shape of the gold locket at her throat.

GABRIEL

(Voice a low growl)

Stop moving. You’ll make it worse.

He doesn’t look back. The words are flat, final.

SCENE 4 — ART GALLERY GALA - LATER

Julian is on his phone, his back to the party. His face is a perfect mask of distress.

JULIAN

(Into phone)

Mr. Arman, it’s Julian. She’s gone… Her security detail can’t find her. Her clutch is still on the table… No, I don’t know. I just stepped away for a moment to close the deal.

He hangs up. He takes a breath, composes himself, and turns to a security guard. A single, perfect tear tracks down his cheek.

JULIAN

My fiancée. She’s missing.

EPISODE END

In the dark van, Gabriel’s phone buzzes. He glances down. A text message illuminates his grim face.

TEXT: NEW DIRECTIVE. ASSET IS A LIABILITY. CLEAN UP.

His jaw tightens. He looks up at the rearview mirror. Leila’s terrified, tear-filled eyes meet his. The reflection shows the endless, dark road ahead.

EPISODE 2: LIABILITY

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The van barrels down a dark highway. Gabriel glances at the text on his phone. His face hardens into stone. He looks in the rearview mirror at Leila, then violently SWERVES the van off the road, tires screaming onto a dark, unmarked exit.

SCENE 1 — INT. VAN - MOVING - NIGHT

Leila is thrown against the door, crying out. The van bumps and rattles down a dirt track, headlights cutting through a tunnel of trees.

LEILA

(panicked)

What are you doing?! Stop!

Gabriel ignores her, his knuckles white on the steering wheel, eyes scanning the darkness ahead.

LEILA

My fiancé will pay you. He’ll give you anything you want, just tell me what this is about!

Gabriel’s eyes flick to the rearview mirror, meeting hers. His voice is flat, cold.

GABRIEL

He already did.

SCENE 2 — INT. JULIAN'S PENTHOUSE OFFICE - NIGHT

Julian stands before a floor-to-ceiling window, a glass of scotch in hand, the city lights glittering below. He speaks calmly into his phone.

JULIAN

The directive was clear. No loose ends. Confirm the operator received the update.

He listens, taking a slow sip. A flicker of annoyance crosses his perfect features.

JULIAN

He’s a professional. He follows orders. But if he deviates… you have your own protocol. Make it look like part of the original tragedy. A ransom exchange gone wrong. The public loves a martyr.

He hangs up. The mask of the grieving fiancé is gone, replaced by chilling, absolute control.

SCENE 3 — EXT. ABANDONED GAS STATION - NIGHT

The van is parked under the single, flickering light of a derelict gas station. The engine is off. The only sound is the chirping of crickets.

Gabriel gets out and opens Leila’s sliding door. He doesn't drag her out. He just stands there.

LEILA

(voice trembling)

What is this place? What’s happening?

GABRIEL

The plan changed.

LEILA

What plan? The ransom?

Gabriel pulls out his phone. He doesn't say a word, just holds it out so she can see the screen.

The text message glows in the dark: `NEW DIRECTIVE. ASSET IS A LIABILITY. CLEAN UP.`

Leila reads it. Her brow furrows in confusion, then her eyes widen in dawning horror. She looks from the phone to his face.

LEILA

Clean up? What does that mean? Who… who sent that?

GABRIEL

It means the people who paid me to take you, now want me to kill you.

The words hang in the air. The truth hits Leila like a physical blow. She clutches the small gold locket at her throat, her breath catching in a sob.

LEILA

(a whisper)

Julian…

EPISODE END

Gabriel watches her, his expression unreadable. He takes a step back from the open van door, creating a space between them.

GABRIEL

They’ll send someone else. Soon. So you have a choice. You can run, try your luck in the dark. Or you can get back in this van, and trust the only person on Earth who can keep you alive.

He waits. The camera holds on Leila’s shattered face, trapped between her kidnapper and the man she was supposed to marry. In the far distance, the faint sound of an approaching engine begins to grow.

EPISODE 3: A DIFFERENT CAGE

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The distant engine noise grows louder, closer. Headlights sweep across the trees. Leila’s eyes dart from the dark road to Gabriel’s unyielding face. She clutches the gold locket at her neck.

SCENE 1 — INT. VAN - NIGHT

The van screeches onto the highway, tires protesting. Leila is slammed back against the cold metal wall. She stares at Gabriel’s profile, illuminated by the passing glow of streetlights.

LEILA

Why? Why would Julian want me dead?

Gabriel’s eyes stay fixed on the road, checking the rearview mirror.

GABRIEL

You tell me. What do you have that he wants?

LEILA

We were getting married. It was a merger. Our families... it was a deal.

GABRIEL

Deals get broken. Assets get liquidated.

Leila flinches at the word "assets." Her breathing is ragged.

LEILA

This is insane. You could be lying. This could be the real ransom demand.

GABRIEL

The man in the woods had a suppressor and a shovel. That’s not for a ransom.

The brutal finality of his words hangs in the air. Leila shrinks back, wrapping her arms around herself. The van speeds into the darkness.

SCENE 2 — INT. GAS STATION RESTROOM - NIGHT

A dirty, flickering fluorescent light hums overhead. Leila stares at her reflection in the cracked, grimy mirror. Her makeup is smeared, her designer dress is torn at the shoulder. She looks like a ghost of herself.

The door creaks open. Gabriel stands there, holding out a bundle of clothes: a worn hoodie, jeans, a baseball cap. He doesn't look at her, his eyes scanning the empty parking lot outside.

GABRIEL

Change. Now. That dress is a beacon.

He places the clothes on the wet counter and turns to leave, pausing at the door.

GABRIEL

And lose the jewelry. All of it.

His eyes flick to the locket in her hand. She instinctively closes her fist around it.

LEILA

No. Not this.

Gabriel’s jaw tightens. He gives a sharp, almost imperceptible nod and closes the door, leaving her alone with the reflection of a stranger.

SCENE 3 — INT. VAN - LATER

Leila sits huddled in the passenger seat, swallowed by the oversized hoodie. The van is parked under a concrete overpass, shielded from view. Rain begins to streak down the windshield. Gabriel is focused on a burner phone, his thumb moving quickly.

LEILA

Who hired you?

He doesn’t look up.

GABRIEL

It doesn’t matter.

LEILA

(voice stronger now)

If it wasn’t Julian directly, it was a cutout. A lawyer? An associate? His name was on the wire transfer, wasn't it? Tell me who paid you to kidnap me.

Gabriel stops typing. He slowly lifts his head, his steel-colored eyes meeting hers.

GABRIEL

The account that paid my advance was in your name.

Leila’s face drains of all color. The burner phone in Gabriel’s hand suddenly buzzes with an incoming message. He glances down at the screen. His expression hardens into something cold and dangerous.

GABRIEL

Damn it.

LEILA

What? What is it?

EPISODE END

Gabriel kills the engine, plunging them into darkness and silence. He looks at her, his voice a low, urgent whisper.

GABRIEL

They put a tracker in the clothes.

EPISODE 4: SECOND SKIN

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The car is plunged into darkness. Leila stares at Gabriel, his face barely visible, his voice a low, urgent whisper.

GABRIEL

They put a tracker in the clothes.

Leila’s breath catches. She looks down at the expensive jacket, the soft cashmere pants. A second skin. A cage.

SCENE 1 — EXT. ABANDONED GAS STATION - NIGHT

The car doors fly open. Gabriel pulls Leila out, his grip firm on her arm. He scans the dark, empty highway.

LEILA

(panicked whisper)

How? How do you know?

Gabriel shoves the burner phone into her line of sight. A single line of text glows on the screen: `ASSET PINGING. CONFIRM VISUAL.`

GABRIEL

They’re close. They think they have us pinned.

Leila frantically pats the pockets of the jacket.

LEILA

I don’t feel anything!

GABRIEL

It won’t be in a pocket. It’s smarter than that.

He grabs the lapel of her jacket, his fingers searching the seams. Leila’s mind races, connecting fragmented pieces of information—security briefings, articles about luxury goods.

LEILA

The tag. In the collar. High-end brands sometimes weave filament trackers into the label itself.

Gabriel doesn’t hesitate. He pulls a small, wicked-looking knife from his boot. He slices the designer label at the nape of the jacket. With the tip of the blade, he pries something out.

A tiny black chip, no bigger than a grain of rice, falls onto the cracked asphalt.

Gabriel crushes it under his heel with a sharp, grinding motion.

GABRIEL

The pants, too. All of it. Now.

SCENE 2 — INT. GAS STATION WASHROOM - NIGHT

The washroom is filthy, the mirror cracked. Gabriel shoves a bundle of worn clothes into Leila’s arms. A faded flannel shirt and a pair of men's cargo pants.

GABRIEL

Change. Leave everything you were wearing on the floor.

Leila freezes. The thought of undressing here, in front of him, is paralyzing. She clutches the clothes to her chest.

LEILA

I can’t—

Gabriel seems to understand. He turns his back to her, facing the grimy door, a silent, unmoving guard.

GABRIEL

You have sixty seconds.

His voice is flat, devoid of emotion, but the gesture is unmistakable. A sliver of trust.

Leila strips out of the designer clothes, her movements clumsy with haste. The cold air bites at her skin. She pulls on the rough fabric. The shirt smells faintly of soap and him. The clothes are huge, swallowing her small frame.

She touches the gold locket at her throat. The only thing that’s still hers.

LEILA

Done.

Gabriel turns around. His eyes flick over her, taking in the change. He nods once, then grabs the pile of expensive clothes from the floor.

SCENE 3 — EXT. ABANDONED GAS STATION - NIGHT

Gabriel shoves the clothes into a rusty trash barrel. He douses them with lighter fluid from a small canister. A match flares. Flames erupt, consuming the fabric in a hungry orange blaze.

They watch the fire for a beat. The only light for miles.

LEILA

My bank account. He couldn’t have accessed it. The security protocols… my father set them up.

Gabriel doesn’t look at her. He’s already moving toward a beat-up pickup truck hidden behind the station, its paint peeling.

GABRIEL

Then your father gave him access. Or Julian is even better than I thought.

He pries open the truck door and slides under the steering wheel. Leila stands by the fire, the horrible implication of his words sinking in.

A moment later, sparks fly from the dashboard. The old engine coughs, sputters, then roars to life.

GABRIEL

(shouts over the engine)

Get in! We’re leaving their ghost behind.

EPISODE END

Leila runs to the truck, pulling herself into the passenger seat. As Gabriel slams his door shut, two brilliant white headlights crest a hill down the highway. The beams slice through the darkness, pinning the truck. They aren't just driving. They're accelerating. Coming right for them.

EPISODE 5: THE GHOST'S PRICE

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The old pickup truck is pinned in the blinding glare of two headlights. The other vehicle is accelerating, its engine a high-pitched snarl, coming straight for them on the empty highway.

SCENE 1 — INT. PICKUP TRUCK - NIGHT

Gabriel doesn't hesitate. He slams the gearshift into reverse, cranking the wheel hard.

GABRIEL

(shouting)

Hold on!

The truck lurches backward, tires screaming on the asphalt. Leila is thrown against the passenger door, her hands braced on the dashboard.

The pursuing car, a sleek black sedan, rockets past where they were just a second ago, its horn blaring.

Gabriel wrenches the wheel again, sending them fishtailing onto the gravel shoulder. The truck shudders to a stop, kicking up a cloud of dust that momentarily obscures the sedan's red taillights as it disappears down the road.

Leila gasps for breath, her heart hammering.

LEILA

They were trying to kill us. They weren't trying to stop us.

Gabriel watches the taillights vanish. His knuckles are white on the steering wheel.

GABRIEL

That was the point.

SCENE 2 — EXT. DIRT ROAD - NIGHT

The truck is parked under the cover of dense trees, miles from the highway. The engine is off. The only sound is crickets.

Gabriel pulls a slim, featureless burner phone from his jacket.

LEILA

Who are you calling? The police?

Gabriel gives a short, mirthless laugh.

GABRIEL

Someone better. And worse.

He scrolls to a single contact: GHOST.

GABRIEL

She can get us clean. New route, new identities. But it comes with a price. Always.

LEILA

What kind of price?

GABRIEL

The kind you don't want to know about until you have to pay it.

He presses the call button. Leila watches him, the absolute certainty in his movements more terrifying than the chase itself.

SCENE 3 — INT. PICKUP TRUCK - NIGHT

Gabriel holds the phone to his ear. His face is a mask of concentration.

GABRIEL

It's me.

A pause as he listens. His eyes scan the dark woods outside the windshield.

GABRIEL

They're on us. Black sedan. Aggressive. How?

He listens again, his jaw tightening.

GABRIEL

Commercial tracker. High-end. Of course. I need a ghost protocol. Full package.

Another pause. He closes his eyes for a fraction of a second.

GABRIEL

I know the terms. Send the drop point. We'll be there.

He ends the call without another word, tossing the phone onto the seat between them.

SCENE 4 — INT. PICKUP TRUCK - NIGHT

Leila stares at the phone, then at Gabriel.

LEILA

What did she say? A tracker?

GABRIEL

She says they aren't following us. They're following you. There's a GPS chip on you somewhere. Small. Probably woven into your clothes, or…

His eyes drift down. Leila follows his gaze. Her hand instinctively flies to her chest, clutching the delicate gold locket her grandmother gave her.

GABRIEL

…or something you’d never think to take off.

Leila’s breath catches in her throat.

GABRIEL

Before we go anywhere, we have to find it. And we have to get rid of it. Now.

EPISODE END

Close on Leila’s fingers, trembling as they tighten around the cold metal of her locket. The one constant thing in her life might be the very thing that gets her killed.

EPISODE 6: THE GOLDEN BEACON

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

Leila’s fingers tremble, tightening around the delicate gold locket at her throat. Gabriel watches her, his face a mask of grim urgency. The air in the dusty room is thick with unspoken fear.

SCENE 1 — ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - DAY

The single lightbulb overhead hums. Dust motes dance in the weak light.

GABRIEL

Take it off.

Leila flinches, her hand protectively covering the locket.

LEILA

No. I can’t.

GABRIEL

That’s not a request. It’s a GPS tracker, Leila. A top-of-the-line microdot. They’re watching every step we take.

LEILA

It was my grandmother’s. It’s all I have left of her.

GABRIEL

(voice dangerously low)

Your grandmother would want you alive. Give it to me.

He takes a step closer. She takes a step back, her back hitting a cold brick wall. Her eyes are wide, defiant.

LEILA

You don’t understand.

GABRIEL

I understand that if you keep that thing on, we’re both dead in an hour. Now take. It. Off.

SCENE 2 — THORNE CORP - PRESS ROOM - DAY

A wall of cameras flash. JULIAN THORNE stands at a podium, his expression a perfect portrait of grief and resolve. He looks exhausted, but impeccably dressed.

JULIAN

(into the microphones)

I want to be clear. My family, the Arman family... we will move heaven and earth. We will spare no expense. Every resource is being deployed to find my fiancée, Leila.

He pauses, letting the weight of his words sink in. He looks directly into the main camera.

JULIAN

To those who have her… if you are watching… there is no corner of the world you can hide in. We will find you. And we will bring her home.

His jaw is set. A single, perfect tear rolls down his cheek.

SCENE 3 — ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - DAY

Leila stares at the locket, now resting in her palm. Gabriel stands over a rusted metal table, a small toolkit laid out.

LEILA

Can’t you just… disable it?

GABRIEL

The transmitter is probably wired to the clasp. Any attempt to force it could send an alert. We have to be surgical.

Leila reluctantly places the locket on the table. Gabriel picks up a pair of fine-tipped pliers. His large, scarred hands are surprisingly steady as he works on the tiny, intricate piece of jewelry.

Leila watches, hugging herself. She’s watching him dismantle the last piece of her old life.

GABRIEL

(without looking up)

He gave it to you, didn’t he? Julian.

LEILA

(voice barely a whisper)

No. My grandmother did. But he had it… repaired. For my birthday last year. The clasp was broken.

Gabriel stops. He looks from the locket to her, his eyes cold with understanding. He carefully pries the backplate off. A minuscule black chip with a blinking red light is nestled inside.

GABRIEL

He didn’t repair it. He weaponized it.

SCENE 4 — ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - DAY

Gabriel holds the tiny tracker between his thumb and forefinger before dropping it into a bottle of water. He screws the cap on tight.

GABRIEL

That’ll confuse the signal long enough for us to get a head start. We leave in five.

Leila nods, clutching the now-empty locket in her hand. A fragile sense of relief washes over her. For the first time in days, she feels a flicker of hope.

Suddenly, a metallic CLICK echoes from the heavy steel door across the warehouse.

Both of them freeze.

The unmistakable sound of a key sliding into the lock.

Gabriel draws his weapon, his body instantly shielding Leila’s. They stare at the door as the lock begins to turn.

EPISODE END

Close on the doorknob, slowly, silently rotating. They are not alone.

EPISODE 7: THE GHOST AT THE DOOR

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The doorknob finishes its turn. The heavy steel door swings inward with a low groan. Gabriel aims his weapon into the darkness beyond.

A lone figure steps through the threshold. Not a hulking mercenary. A woman.

SCENE 1 — WAREHOUSE - CONTINUOUS

The woman is lean, dressed in dark, functional gear. Her face is sharp, her eyes missing nothing. She raises her hands, palms open, a gesture of peace that doesn't match the coldness in her gaze.

ANYA

Easy, G. Wouldn't want you to do something you'd regret. Again.

Gabriel doesn’t lower his weapon. His jaw is tight. Leila peeks out from behind him, clutching her locket.

GABRIEL

Anya. What are you doing here?

ANYA

Saving your ass. Julian Thorne just tripled the bounty. Open contract, untraceable crypto. Every bottom-feeder from here to the coast is crawling out of the woodwork for a piece of you. And the girl.

Anya’s eyes flick to Leila, assessing her for a brief, dismissive moment.

ANYA

(to Gabriel)

This place is burned. You’ve got an hour, maybe less.

SCENE 2 — WAREHOUSE - LATER

Anya stands by a small laptop, the screen glowing with lines of code. Gabriel watches her, his weapon now holstered but his stance still rigid. Leila stands apart, trying to follow the clipped, coded exchange.

GABRIEL

How did you find us?

ANYA

You still use the same emergency protocols. Predictable. That's what got your last team killed, remember?

A muscle jumps in Gabriel’s cheek. Leila flinches at the casual cruelty of Anya’s words.

GABRIEL

I need an exit. Clean.

ANYA

I have one. A sterile vehicle, four blocks north. It’ll get you out of the city grid. But it’s not free. You know how this works.

GABRIEL

What’s the price?

ANYA

I’ll call it in when I need it. And you’ll answer. No questions.

Leila watches Gabriel. Sees the conflict in his eyes. He’s trading one danger for another. He gives a single, sharp nod.

GABRIEL

Done.

SCENE 3 — WAREHOUSE - MOMENTS LATER

Anya has vanished back into the night. Gabriel shoves a water bottle and a small medkit into a worn backpack. Leila approaches him cautiously.

LEILA

Who was she?

Gabriel doesn’t look at her. He continues packing.

GABRIEL

A ghost.

LEILA

She said… she said your last team was killed. What did she mean?

He stops. Turns to face her. His eyes are like steel shutters coming down.

GABRIEL

It means the past stays buried. It means you need to focus on right now. We move in two minutes.

He turns away, shutting down the conversation. Leila is left staring at his back, the space between them suddenly feeling colder and more dangerous than the threat outside.

EPISODE END

Gabriel grabs the pack and heads for a side exit Anya indicated. He pauses at the door, listening. He turns back to Leila, his voice a low, urgent whisper.

GABRIEL

Stay close. And no more questions.

He pushes the door open a crack, peering into the rain-slicked alley beyond.

EPISODE 8: THE ALLEY

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

Rain lashes a narrow, trash-strewn alley. Gabriel pulls Leila through the open door, his hand clamped firmly on her arm. He shoves the door closed behind them, the latch clicking with grim finality.

SCENE 1 — EXT. ALLEY - NIGHT

The alley is a canyon of wet brick and overflowing dumpsters. A single flickering bulb overhead casts long, dancing shadows.

Gabriel presses Leila against the wall, his body shielding hers. He scans the mouth of the alley.

GABRIEL

(Whispering)

Down there. End of the block. Move.

He starts to pull her along. Her expensive shoes slip on the slick, greasy pavement. She stumbles, catching herself on his arm.

LEILA

I can’t—

GABRIEL

You will.

Headlights sweep across the alley entrance. Gabriel reacts instantly, shoving Leila into the deep shadow of a dumpster. He presses in close, his breath warm against her ear. The car passes without slowing.

GABRIEL

(Low, intense)

They’re circling the block. We have ninety seconds.

He doesn't wait for a reply, just grabs her hand and pulls her into a dead run.

SCENE 2 — INT. PARKING GARAGE - NIGHT

They burst through a fire exit into the echoing quiet of a multi-level parking garage. The air is cold, smelling of concrete and exhaust fumes. They are both soaked, shivering.

Leila leans against a concrete pillar, gasping for breath. Gabriel is already moving, scanning the rows of cars.

LEILA

Where are we going? What now?

Gabriel ignores her, stopping by an old, nondescript sedan. He pulls a small tool from his pocket.

GABRIEL

Get in.

LEILA

You’re stealing a car?

GABRIEL

I’m borrowing it. Get in the passenger side. Stay low.

He works at the lock. A sharp click. The door opens. He slides into the driver's seat and begins working on the ignition wires beneath the steering column. Leila gets in, huddling down in her seat.

LEILA

You do this a lot?

The engine sputters, then roars to life. Gabriel kills the headlights.

GABRIEL

Too much.

SCENE 3 — INT. SEDAN - NIGHT

Gabriel drives without lights, navigating the dark city streets with practiced ease. Leila watches his profile, illuminated only by the faint glow of the dashboard. He pulls a burner phone from his pack and dials a number.

GABRIEL

(Into phone)

It’s me.

A tinny, distorted voice responds, inaudible to Leila.

GABRIEL

Anya’s nest is blown. I need a new one. Clean. Deep.

He listens, his jaw tight.

GABRIEL

I know what it costs. I’m calling in the marker from Istanbul. The whole thing.

Leila flinches at the mention of Istanbul. She watches him, seeing the weight of his past settle on him.

GABRIEL

The package is with me. High value. Yes, it’s her.

Another pause. Gabriel’s knuckles are white on the steering wheel.

GABRIEL

What do you mean, ‘new directive’?

EPISODE END

Gabriel’s face is a mask of cold fury. He listens to the voice on the phone, his eyes fixed on the rain-streaked windshield ahead.

GABRIEL

(Into phone, dangerously quiet)

Say that again.

The tinny voice crackles. Gabriel’s gaze flicks to Leila in the passenger seat, a new, terrifying understanding dawning in his eyes. He ends the call without saying goodbye.

LEILA

Gabriel? What is it?

GABRIEL

The contract’s changed. It’s not about you anymore. It’s about us.

EPISODE 9: TARGET PAIR

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The car’s interior is lit only by the frantic swipe of the windshield wipers. Leila stares at Gabriel, his face a grim silhouette. The weight of his last words hangs between them.

SCENE 1 — INT. CAR - NIGHT

Rain lashes against the glass. Gabriel grips the steering wheel, knuckles white, scanning the dark, wet streets.

LEILA

(Voice trembling)

Us? What do you mean, ‘us’?

GABRIEL

The people who hired me… they don’t like loose ends. I’m a loose end now.

LEILA

Because you didn’t…

She can’t finish the sentence. The implication is too monstrous.

GABRIEL

Because I didn’t follow the final directive. No witnesses.

He takes a hard right, the tires squealing on the slick pavement. Leila flinches, grabbing the dashboard. The horror of her situation crashes down on her in a new, terrifying wave. Julian didn't just want her gone. He wanted her erased. And now, the man who saved her is marked for death, too.

LEILA

So we’re running from your employers? And from Julian?

GABRIEL

They’re one and the same now. We need to disappear.

SCENE 2 — EXT. ROADSIDE MOTEL - LATER

A flickering neon sign reads "OAS S M TEL," the letters buzzing miserably in the rain. Gabriel pulls the battered sedan into a dark corner of the parking lot, killing the engine.

He turns to Leila, pushing a wad of damp cash into her hand.

GABRIEL

One room. Two beds. Pay cash. Use a fake name, something forgettable. Don’t look them in the eye, but don’t look away. Just act tired.

Leila stares at the peeling paint of the motel office, then back at the money. This is a world away from the five-star hotels of her past.

LEILA

What if they ask for ID?

GABRIEL

Tell them you lost your wallet. You’re just passing through. Be convincing.

He watches her, his gaze intense. It’s not a request. It’s a test. Leila takes a shaky breath, nods, and tucks her locket inside her shirt. She gets out of the car, pulling her torn jacket tight, and walks toward the dim light of the office.

SCENE 3 — INT. MOTEL ROOM - NIGHT

The room smells of stale smoke and disinfectant. A single lamp casts long shadows. The floral bedspreads are faded and thin.

Leila sits on the edge of one bed, watching Gabriel. He’s methodically checking his weapon on the small table, his movements economical and precise.

LEILA

Who was on the phone?

GABRIEL

(Without looking up)

A ghost. Someone who warns me when the storm changes direction.

LEILA

And it’s changed.

GABRIEL

It’s a hurricane now. And we’re in the middle of it.

He finishes with the gun and stands, moving to the window. He pulls the grimy curtain back a fraction of an inch, peering out into the rain-swept darkness.

LEILA

We can’t keep running forever.

GABRIEL

Forever’s not the goal. Surviving the next five minutes is.

EPISODE END

A low rumble grows louder. The sound of a heavy engine. Headlights sweep across the parking lot, flashing through the gap in the curtains and painting the room in a stark, momentary glare. The engine cuts out. Right outside their door.

Gabriel spins away from the window, his face a mask of lethal focus. He raises his weapon.

GABRIEL

(Low, urgent)

Down. Get down now.

EPISODE 10: THE KNOCK AT THE DOOR

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The motel room is plunged into darkness, then lit by a blinding sweep of headlights. An engine cuts out. Silence. Gabriel raises his weapon, his face a mask of lethal focus.

GABRIEL

(Low, urgent)

Down. Get down now.

SCENE 1 — MOTEL ROOM - NIGHT

Leila drops to the floor behind the flimsy bed, clutching her locket. The springs groan in protest. Gabriel moves like a shadow to the door, pressing his ear against the cheap wood.

He risks a glance through the peephole. The distorted lens shows only the opposite door, the parking lot beyond empty in the small circle of vision.

LEILA

(Whispering)

Who is it? Can you see?

GABRIEL

Stay quiet.

Footsteps crunch on gravel. One person. Slow, deliberate. They stop directly in front of their door. The silence stretches, thick and suffocating.

Then, a sharp KNOCK. Three quick raps.

Leila flinches, her breath catching in her throat. Gabriel doesn’t move a muscle, gun held steady, aimed at the door.

SCENE 2 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

The knock comes again, louder this time. A man’s voice, muffled through the door. It’s calm, almost bored.

MAN (O.S.)

Management. Just checking on a noise complaint.

Gabriel’s eyes narrow. He shakes his head almost imperceptibly at Leila. A noise complaint at this hour, in a place like this? It’s a lie.

LEILA

(Mouths the word)

Trap.

GABRIEL

(Whispering)

They’re testing. Seeing if the room is occupied.

He backs away from the door, moving to the side wall, out of the direct line of fire. He gestures for Leila to stay down, to move further into the corner.

The handle jiggles. A metallic scrape. A keycard sliding into the electronic lock.

A soft BEEP, followed by a CLICK as the lock disengages.

SCENE 3 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

The door swings inward with a low creak.

A man stands in the doorway, silhouetted against the parking lot lights. He’s older, maybe sixty, with a tired face and a rumpled suit. He doesn’t look like a killer. He looks like a weary traveler.

He holds his empty hands up, palms out.

GABRIEL

Silas? What the hell are you doing here?

Gabriel keeps his gun trained on the man, SILAS, but his voice is laced with disbelief.

SILAS

Cleaning up your mess, Gabriel. As usual. You’re getting sloppy.

LEILA

(From behind the bed)

Who is he?

GABRIEL

(To Leila)

Stay there.

(To Silas)

How did you find me?

Silas steps inside, letting the door click shut behind him. He ignores the gun.

SILAS

The people you’re running from? They aren’t subtle. They left a digital trail a child could follow. I just got here first. You need to see this.

SCENE 4 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

Silas pulls a slim tablet from his jacket pocket. He taps the screen. It glows to life.

SILAS

Julian Thorne isn’t just hunting you anymore. He’s changed the game.

He turns the tablet so Gabriel and Leila can see. Leila cautiously peers over the edge of the mattress.

On the screen is a live video feed. A well-appointed study. A woman is tied to a chair. It’s ELARA, Leila’s grandmother’s fiercely loyal, elderly personal assistant. A man in a dark suit stands behind her, a hand on her shoulder.

Leila gasps, a hand flying to her mouth. Her eyes are wide with horror.

GABRIEL

What is this?

SILAS

A message. Sent to your father an hour ago. The feed is live. Thorne is making this personal.

EPISODE END

The camera on the tablet zooms in on Elara’s terrified face. A tear traces a path down her wrinkled cheek. Leila stares, frozen, realizing the cage she escaped just got infinitely larger, trapping everyone she ever cared about.

EPISODE 11: THE PERSONAL MESSAGE

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The tablet screen shows ELARA, Leila’s elderly nanny, terrified. A man in a suit stands behind her. Leila’s hand is clamped over her mouth, a choked sob escaping.

SCENE 1 — SILAS’S HIDEOUT - CONTINUOUS

The tablet sits on the metal table, the live feed a sickening loop of Elara’s silent fear.

LEILA

(whispering)

Elara... No. This is my fault. He’s doing this because of me.

Gabriel grabs the tablet, his eyes scanning every pixel of the image.

GABRIEL

Silas, can you trace this? Location, anything?

SILAS

(Shakes his head)

It’s a ghost feed. Bounced through a dozen dead drops. By the time we find the source, he’ll be long gone. This isn't about us finding her.

Leila looks up, her eyes blazing with a mixture of terror and fury.

LEILA

It’s a leash. He’s showing me he can pull it whenever he wants.

GABRIEL

He’s showing you he can get to anyone you care about. He wants you scared. He wants you to make a mistake.

LEILA

He already made his.

SCENE 2 — SILAS’S HIDEOUT - LATER

Leila paces the concrete floor, her movements sharp, agitated. She clutches the locket at her neck. Gabriel watches her, leaning against a wall.

GABRIEL

Panicking won’t help her.

LEILA

I’m not panicking. I’m thinking.

(She stops dead)

The painting. Behind her. On the wall.

Gabriel picks up the tablet again, zooming in on the background of the video. A dark, ornate oil painting is partially visible.

GABRIEL

What about it? Looks like a thousand other rich-guy paintings.

LEILA

It’s not. It’s a Snyders. The Lion Hunt. My father tried to buy it at auction three years ago. Julian’s father outbid him. It hangs in the west wing of the Thorne family’s old vineyard estate. I’ve seen it once. I know exactly where she is.

Gabriel stares at her, a flicker of surprise in his steel-grey eyes.

GABRIEL

You’re sure?

LEILA

He’s arrogant. He’s using his own property. He never thought I’d be smart enough to notice.

SCENE 3 — SILAS’S HIDEOUT - NIGHT

Gabriel is in a corner, speaking low into a burner phone. Silas is cleaning medical tools nearby, pointedly ignoring the call.

GABRIEL

Ghost, I need satellite imagery. Thorne Vineyard Estate, off Route 9. West wing. Now.

(A beat)

I know what it costs. Just do it.

Across the room, Leila sits at the table. She’s sketching furiously on a piece of scrap paper with a charcoal pencil from Silas’s kit. Her hand moves with practiced speed, her face a mask of concentration.

She finishes, pushing the paper across the table just as Gabriel ends his call.

LEILA

Here. This is the room. The windows, the door… everything I remember.

Gabriel picks up the sketch. It’s a detailed architectural drawing of the room, rendered from memory. His eyes lock onto one specific detail she’s drawn on the far wall, a section with no windows and an unusual seam around the frame of the painting.

GABRIEL

This wall… the trim you drew here. It’s reinforced.

LEILA

It’s just how I remember it. Why?

EPISODE END

Gabriel looks from the drawing to Leila, his expression grim.

GABRIEL

Because that’s not a wall. It’s a vault door. He isn’t just holding Elara there. He’s hiding something else.

EPISODE 12: THE GHOST'S PRICE

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

Leila stares at the drawing, then at Gabriel, her face pale. The safe house feels suddenly colder.

LEILA

A vault? Julian wouldn’t… He wouldn’t lock his own sister in a vault.

SCENE 1 — INT. SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT

Gabriel paces the small room, his energy a coiled spring. Leila sits at the table, clutching the pencil.

GABRIEL

He would if he was hiding something more valuable than her. That room isn’t a prison. It’s a display case. Elara is just the guard dog.

LEILA

Guard dog for what? His money? His company files?

She shakes her head, frustrated, trying to piece it together.

LEILA

It doesn’t make sense. He has offshore accounts, encrypted servers for all of that. He’s meticulous.

GABRIEL

Exactly. So it’s not digital. It’s something physical. Something he needs close. Something he can’t afford to lose, no matter what.

Leila’s eyes go distant, a memory flickering.

LEILA

He once told me the Thorne family legacy wasn’t built on what the world sees… but on what it doesn’t. He called it his “failsafe.”

SCENE 2 — INT. JULIAN'S PENTHOUSE OFFICE - DAY

Julian stands before a floor-to-ceiling window overlooking the city. He’s on a video call on a tablet, his reflection cool and composed.

JULIAN

The perimeter is secure? No anomalies?

SECURITY HEAD (V.O.)

(Tinny, through tablet)

None, sir. The asset is stable.

JULIAN

I’m not asking about the asset’s stability. I’m asking about its security. The container. Is it sealed?

SECURITY HEAD (V.O.)

Air-tight, Mr. Thorne. No one gets in or out without your direct authorization.

JULIAN

Good. Keep it that way. The girl is secondary. The container is everything.

He ends the call, his expression unreadable as he stares out at his empire.

SCENE 3 — INT. SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT

Gabriel sits before a rugged laptop, lines of code scrolling across the screen. An encrypted chat window is open. Leila stands behind him, watching.

LEILA

Can you get in?

GABRIEL

Their security is military-grade. But every system has a ghost. I’m trying to find one.

He types furiously. A new message pops into the chat window from a contact named ‘GHOST’.

GHOST: Thorne Estate. Vault schematics are a dead end. But I found a maintenance backdoor. Biometric. Needs two authorized signals simultaneously.

Gabriel’s fingers hover over the keyboard.

GABRIEL

Two signals… Julian and who else?

LEILA

His head of security. Marcus. They’re never in the same place unless it’s an emergency.

Another message from GHOST appears.

GHOST: I can clone their biometric keys. But it’s loud. You’ll have a 90-second window before every alarm on the eastern seaboard goes off.

Gabriel lets out a sharp breath.

GABRIEL

Ninety seconds.

LEILA

Is that enough?

The final message from GHOST appears, stark and demanding.

GHOST: My price for the keys: The Arman family’s private ledger. All of it. You have one hour to deliver it to my drop, or the backdoor vanishes forever.

EPISODE END

Gabriel looks from the screen to Leila, his face grim. He just traded one impossible situation for another.

EPISODE 13: THE PRICE OF KEYS

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The glow of the laptop screen illuminates Leila’s horrified face. Gabriel stands over her, his expression a mask of grim intensity. The demand from GHOST is stark, unblinking.

LEILA

(whispering)

The private ledger... No. It’s impossible.

GABRIEL

Impossible died an hour ago. We have fifty-eight minutes left.

SCENE 1 — MOTEL ROOM - NIGHT

The room is cheap, anonymous. The air is thick with the smell of stale coffee and fear. Leila pushes back from the laptop, shaking her head.

LEILA

You don’t understand. That ledger isn’t just about money. It’s a record of every secret, every deal, every... compromise my family has ever made. Releasing it would destroy them.

GABRIEL

They left you for dead in a shipping container. I’d say the family is already destroyed.

He yanks a chair over, sitting opposite her, leaning in close. His voice is low, urgent.

GABRIEL

(CONT'D)

This isn’t a negotiation. It’s a transaction. Ghost wants the ledger. We want the keys to that server farm. This is the only way we get to Julian. The only way you live.

LEILA

My father would be ruined. Hunted.

GABRIEL

He’s not the one with a kill order on his head right now. Are you with me or not?

Leila clutches the locket at her throat. Her eyes meet his, a storm of conflict within them. She gives a single, sharp nod.

SCENE 2 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

Gabriel watches, tense, as Leila’s fingers fly across the keyboard of the burner laptop. She navigates a series of arcane security prompts.

GABRIEL

What is that?

LEILA

It’s not a simple password. It’s a catechism. Questions only family would know.

A prompt appears on screen: WHERE DOES THE WEEPING LADY WATCH THE SEA?

LEILA

(muttering to herself)

The Rodin sculpture at the Biarritz estate. The one grandmother hated.

She types. Another prompt: WHAT WAS THE NAME OF THE FIRST DEBT PAID?

LEILA

(a bitter laugh)

Constantine. The shipping magnate father drove into bankruptcy in ‘98. He named a yacht after him. Sick joke.

She types again. Her face is pale. Each question is a ghost from her past, a reminder of the gilded cage she never truly saw.

GABRIEL

Twenty minutes left, Leila.

LEILA

I know.

A final prompt appears. WHAT IS THE PROMISE OF THE LOCKET?

Leila freezes. Her hand goes to her neck.

GABRIEL

What is it?

LEILA

It’s from my grandmother. The inscription.

She fumbles with the clasp, her hands trembling. She opens the small gold heart.

SCENE 3 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

CLOSE ON LOCKET - An inscription reads: Semper ad veritatem. Always toward the truth.

Leila types the phrase. The screen flickers, then resolves into a dense, encrypted spreadsheet. Lines of code, account numbers, names. A web of immense, dark power.

LEILA

My God.

She stares, mesmerized and repulsed. The scale of it is breathtaking. It’s worse than she ever imagined.

GABRIEL

Don’t read it. Just send it.

LEILA

This will burn everything to the ground.

GABRIEL

Good. Sometimes that’s what it takes to see clearly. Now.

He points to the screen. She hesitates for a split second, then her jaw tightens. She drags the file into a transfer window and hits SEND. A progress bar appears, crawling from 0%.

SCENE 4 — MOTEL ROOM - CONTINUOUS

They watch the progress bar in silence. 34%... 51%... 78%... The only sound is the hum of the old refrigerator and their own ragged breathing.

Suddenly, a red banner flashes across the top of the screen.

ALERT: UNAUTHORIZED ACCESS DETECTED. SYSTEM LOCKDOWN IN 60 SECONDS. LOCATION TRACE INITIATED.

GABRIEL

Damn it. Julian’s people.

The progress bar hits 96%. The laptop fan whirs frantically.

LEILA

It’s not going to make it.

GABRIEL

It has to.

98%... 99%... The bar hangs there for an agonizing eternity. Then, it vanishes. TRANSFER COMPLETE.

A new message from GHOST pops up instantly: KEYS SENT. GOOD LUCK. YOU'LL NEED IT.

At the exact same moment—

The unmistakable sound of tires screeching to a halt on the gravel just outside their door.

EPISODE END

Gabriel grabs his pistol and the laptop bag, pulling Leila toward the flimsy bathroom window. The motel room door splinters, kicked open with brutal force. They are trapped.

EPISODE 14: THE GHOST'S KEY

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The flimsy bathroom window shatters as Gabriel smashes it with the butt of his pistol. He shoves Leila toward the opening, his body shielding her from the splintered motel room door.

SCENE 1 — MOTEL BATHROOM - NIGHT

A heavy boot connects with the main door again. CRACK. Wood splinters.

GABRIEL

Go! Now!

Leila scrambles through the jagged opening, cutting her arm on a shard of glass. She lands hard on the damp ground outside.

Gabriel turns, firing two precise shots into the main room, not to kill, but to slow them down. The shadows of two armed men recoil.

He vaults through the window after Leila, grabbing her arm and pulling her to her feet.

GABRIEL

Don't look back. Run.

They plunge into the darkness of the woods behind the motel.

SCENE 2 — WOODS BEHIND MOTEL - NIGHT

They move fast, branches whipping at their faces. The sounds of shouting and car doors slamming fade behind them. Leila stumbles, gasping for breath. Gabriel steadies her, his grip firm.

LEILA

(Whispering)

How did they find us?

GABRIEL

Doesn't matter. They did.

He keeps scanning their surroundings, his eyes piercing the gloom.

GABRIEL

The car Ghost sent is two blocks north. A public lot. We just have to get there.

Leila nods, clutching the locket at her throat. She pushes herself to keep pace, the adrenaline overriding her fear.

SCENE 3 — PUBLIC PARKING LOT - NIGHT

Under the flickering orange glow of a single streetlamp, rows of cars sit silent. Gabriel pulls out his phone, the screen illuminating his tense face. An app shows a simple map.

He points the phone at a beat-up, dark blue sedan. The car’s lights flash once. A soft click echoes in the night.

They slide inside, the worn fabric of the seats a small comfort. For a moment, there is only the sound of their ragged breathing.

Gabriel doesn't start the engine. He pulls the laptop from his bag and flips it open.

LEILA

What are you doing? We need to go.

GABRIEL

We need to know what we're running from.

His fingers fly across the trackpad, opening the files he just downloaded. He clicks on a folder labeled ‘ASSET LIQUIDATION.’

SCENE 4 — INSIDE THE CAR - NIGHT

Gabriel’s face is grim. He turns the laptop toward Leila. On the screen is a financial ledger. A wire transfer for a massive sum.

The sender: a shell corporation. The recipient: an offshore account. In the memo line, two words.

LEILA

(Reading aloud, her voice trembling)

“Arman Disposal.”

The truth hits her like a physical blow. This wasn't a ransom. It was an execution order. Signed and paid for by Julian.

GABRIEL

He never wanted you back, Leila.

Tears well in her eyes, but she blinks them back, her grief hardening into something else. Something cold.

LEILA

Show me the rest.

Gabriel nods, scrolling deeper into the files. Encrypted emails. Timelines. Photos of contacts. He stops on a grainy surveillance photo of a man in a suit handing a briefcase to another figure.

Leila leans closer to the screen. Her breath catches in her throat. Her face drains of all color.

LEILA

Wait. Go back.

Gabriel scrolls back to the photo. A close-up on the man in the suit.

LEILA

I know him.

EPISODE END

Close on Leila’s face, a mask of pure shock and betrayal as she stares at the image of a man she trusted implicitly.

EPISODE 15: THE GHOST IN THE SYSTEM

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The laptop screen glows in the dim room. A grainy surveillance photo of a man in a suit. Leila’s face is pale, her eyes wide with disbelief.

LEILA

Marcus. That’s Marcus Vance.

SCENE 1 — SAFE HOUSE / LIVING AREA

Gabriel stands over her, his expression grim. The photo remains on the screen, an indictment.

GABRIEL

Who is he?

LEILA

(voice trembling)

Head of my family’s security. For twenty years. He… he practically raised me. He was at every birthday party, every recital.

She traces the screen with a finger, not quite touching it.

LEILA

My father trusts him more than anyone.

GABRIEL

Which means Julian doesn't just have money. He has the entire Arman security playbook. Every protocol, every asset. He knows how your father would search for you.

Leila looks up at him, the full horror dawning on her.

LEILA

He doesn't just know how my father would search. He’s the one leading the search.

SCENE 2 — SAFE HOUSE / BEDROOM

Minutes later. Gabriel shoves gear into a duffel bag with brutal efficiency. A burner phone, a weapon, a medkit. Leila stands frozen in the doorway, clutching her locket.

GABRIEL

We have to move. Now. If Vance is in Julian's pocket, this location is burned. Every contact I have could be compromised.

LEILA

I remember… last Christmas. He gave me a security briefing. A gift, he called it. A new panic button. He said, "No matter where you are, Leila, I will find you."

Her voice breaks. It wasn't a promise. It was a threat.

GABRIEL

What else? Think. Habits, locations. Anything he wouldn't report to Julian.

LEILA

He’s meticulous. By the book. His own book. He despises loose ends.

Gabriel zips the bag, his eyes locking on hers.

GABRIEL

We’re the loosest end he’s ever had.

SCENE 3 — ALLEYWAY / NIGHT

They hurry down a dark, narrow alley slick with rain. The city's glow reflects off the wet brick. Leila pulls her thin jacket tighter.

LEILA

He has a blind spot.

Gabriel glances at her, not breaking stride.

GABRIEL

Everyone does.

LEILA

His pride. He designed all of my family's emergency protocols himself. He thinks they're flawless. He’d never believe someone could use them against him.

GABRIEL

Go on.

LEILA

Protocol Chimera. It’s a deep cover failsafe. For creating a ghost identity if a family member is compromised on foreign soil. Only three people know the activation code. My father, me… and Marcus.

SCENE 4 — INSIDE A MOVING CAR

They drive in a beat-up sedan, the city lights a blur. Gabriel is at the wheel, his knuckles white. Leila stares out the window, her reflection a ghostly image.

A burner phone on the dashboard BUZZES. A single text message appears.

GHOST: VANCE IS ACTIVE ON THE GRID. HE ACCESSED A PRIVATE FLIGHT MANIFEST. MIAMI TO GENEVA.

Leila turns from the window.

LEILA

Geneva? Why?

GABRIEL

It's not a place. It's a code.

Before he can explain, his eyes flick to the rearview mirror. He says nothing.

Leila follows his gaze. Two pinpricks of light grow steadily brighter, closer. A black SUV, sleek and menacing, weaves through the sparse traffic behind them. It has no plates.

EPISODE END

Close on the black SUV in the rearview mirror, gaining on them with unnerving speed. They’ve been found.

EPISODE 16: THE GHOST

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The black SUV fills the rearview mirror, its grille a predator’s snarl. It surges forward, ramming the back of their sedan with a deafening CRUNCH of metal.

SCENE 1 — INT. GABRIEL'S CAR - NIGHT

The car lurches violently. Leila braces herself against the dashboard, her knuckles white.

LEILA

They’re not trying to stop us, they’re trying to kill us!

Gabriel fights the wheel, his face a mask of concentration. He yanks the car into a sharp right turn, tires screaming.

GABRIEL

Hold on.

He floors it down a narrow side street. The SUV follows, its headlights flooding their car, erasing the shadows.

LEILA

You said Geneva was a code. A code for what?

GABRIEL

For who. A contact. Our only way out of this.

LEILA

Can you lose them?

GABRIEL

(glancing in the mirror)

No. They're too good. We need to disappear.

He pulls a burner phone from the glove compartment with one hand, tossing it to Leila.

GABRIEL

Unlock it. Code is 8-6-4-2. Find the contact named ‘Ghost.’

SCENE 2 — INT. GABRIEL'S CAR - CONTINUOUS

Leila’s fingers tremble as she taps in the code. The SUV bumps them again, harder this time. The rear window spiders with cracks.

LEILA

I have it. What do I do?

GABRIEL

Press call. Put it on speaker. Don't say my name. Don't say yours.

Leila hits the button. A single, tinny ring, then a click. A distorted, electronic female voice answers.

GHOST (V.O.)

You're thirty seconds late. That costs extra.

GABRIEL

(swerving to avoid a dumpster)

Circumstances. We have a tail. Heavy ordinance. No plates.

GHOST (V.O.)

I see you. Two blocks ahead, take the service alley on your left. It’s a dead end.

LEILA

A dead end? She wants us to trap ourselves!

GABRIEL

Do it!

He trusts the voice. He wrenches the wheel, plunging the car into a dark, graffiti-covered alley.

SCENE 3 — EXT. INDUSTRIAL ALLEY - NIGHT

The car screeches to a halt just feet from a brick wall. The engine idles, the only sound in the sudden, claustrophobic quiet. The headlights of the SUV appear at the mouth of the alley, blocking their only exit.

GHOST (V.O.)

They think they have you boxed in. They’re wrong. You see the steel roll-up door on your right?

Leila squints into the darkness. She sees a large, corrugated metal door, part of an old warehouse.

LEILA

Yes. It’s closed.

GHOST (V.O.)

Not for long. The price for this door is a data retrieval. Zurich. High-risk. You in?

Gabriel doesn’t hesitate. The SUV begins to creep down the alley toward them.

GABRIEL

We’re in.

GHOST (V.O.)

Stand by.

SCENE 4 — INT. GABRIEL'S CAR - CONTINUOUS

A loud CLANG echoes through the alley. A heavy locking mechanism on the steel door retracts. Then, with a low groan, the door begins to slowly rise, revealing the pitch-black interior of the warehouse.

The SUV accelerates, its engine roaring, ready to pin them against the wall.

GABRIEL

It’s too slow!

GHOST (V.O.)

Then go faster.

Gabriel slams the car into reverse, then whips it forward, aiming directly for the small, growing gap under the rising door.

EPISODE END

Close on the speedometer needle climbing as Gabriel floors it, the car hurtling towards the narrow opening while the massive steel door continues its agonizingly slow ascent. They have seconds before impact.

EPISODE 17: THE PRICE OF FREEDOM

Duration: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN

The SUV’s engine screams. Metal shrieks against metal as the vehicle scrapes through the impossibly narrow gap under the rising warehouse door. Sparks fly. The world is a blur of speed and noise.

SCENE 1 — INT. SUV - NIGHT

The SUV fishtails onto a deserted industrial road, tires smoking. Gabriel wrestles with the wheel, his knuckles white. Leila is braced against the passenger door, breathing in ragged gasps.

The side mirror is gone, the passenger side of the vehicle a long, deep gash of raw metal.

GABRIEL

(Into his comms)

We’re clear. Status.

GHOST (V.O.)

(Distorted, calm)

For now. They’ll be tracking the vehicle’s plates within minutes. You have a ten-minute window. Ditch the car at the coordinates I’m sending.

A map appears on the dashboard display.

LEILA

(Voice trembling)

Who is that?

GABRIEL

The reason we’re not dead. Now hold on.

He cranks the wheel, swerving down a dark alleyway, the damaged car groaning in protest.

SCENE 2 — INT. SUBWAY TUNNEL - NIGHT

Dripping water echoes in a disused service tunnel. A single bare bulb casts long shadows. Gabriel works quickly, prying the license plates off the abandoned SUV with a tire iron.

Leila stands watch, clutching her locket. She’s smudged with grease and dirt, but her eyes are sharp, alert.

LEILA

You owe her. Whoever she is.

Gabriel stops, looks at her. He doesn’t deny it.

GABRIEL

Debts in my world aren’t paid with cash.

LEILA

What do they cost?

Gabriel tosses a mangled license plate into a puddle with a splash. He turns back to the car without answering.

GABRIEL

Let’s go. We’re exposed here.

He grabs their go-bag. Leila follows him deeper into the darkness of the tunnel, the sound of their footsteps swallowed by the gloom.

SCENE 3 — INT. SAFE HOUSE ROOM - NIGHT

A sterile, small room. A single mattress on the floor, a folding table with a ruggedized laptop. It feels like a concrete box.

Gabriel sits at the table, the laptop open. On the screen, a heavily pixelated, voice-modulated figure—GHOST.

GHOST (V.O.)

The warehouse team was Thorne’s private security. Off-the-books. He’s escalating. You’re out of places to run.

GABRIEL

So you’re calling in the marker.

GHOST (V.O.)

I pulled you out of the fire. Now, you’re going to walk into another one for me. Julian Thorne is bidding on a piece of hardware at a private auction. A next-gen data encryption key.

GABRIEL

You want me to steal it.

GHOST (V.O.)

I want you to acquire it. The seller is a black marketeer named Silas. The auction is in two days. At the Blackwood Reserve.

Gabriel freezes. He glances over his shoulder. Leila is standing in the doorway, having heard everything. Her face is pale.

LEILA

The Blackwood? That’s impossible. Security there is… it’s a fortress.

GHOST (V.O.)

Which is why you’re the perfect key. Julian will be there. And he’ll never expect to see you.

SCENE 4 — INT. SAFE HOUSE ROOM - LATER

Gabriel has closed the laptop. The room is silent except for the hum of a ventilation fan. Leila stares at him, her fear hardening into resolve.

LEILA

She’s right. He won’t.

GABRIEL

No. It’s too dangerous. I’ll handle it.

LEILA

How? You can’t walk in the front door. I can. I’ve been to a dozen events there. I know the staff, the layout, the blind spots in the surveillance. I know Julian’s tells when he’s nervous.

GABRIEL

They want you dead, Leila. Walking in there is suicide.

LEILA

Hiding in basements waiting for Julian’s men to find us is suicide. This is the first time we can go on the offensive. This is the first time I can fight back.

She steps closer, her eyes blazing with an intensity he’s never seen before.

LEILA

You need me. And I need to do this.

Ghost sends a new file to the laptop. Gabriel opens it. It’s a detailed schematic of the Blackwood Reserve’s main ballroom and vault.

EPISODE END

Close on Leila’s face, illuminated by the laptop screen. She leans in, tracing a path through the digital blueprint with her finger, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination.

EPISODE 18 — The Ghost's Echo

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

[Leila stares at the laptop screen, the schematic of the Blackwood Reserve’s ballroom and vault glowing on her face. Her finger traces a path through the digital blueprint, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination.]

SCENE 1 — THE IMPOSSIBLE PLAN

INT. HIDDEN SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT

LEILA

(Whispering)

This is insane. It's too big. Too many variables.

Gabriel watches her, his expression unreadable. He gestures to a specific section of the blueprint.

GABRIEL

The vault. That's the target. Everything else is a distraction.

Leila shakes her head, still tracing lines on the screen.

LEILA

A distraction that could get us killed. Or worse, get you killed.

[Gabriel steps closer, his gaze intense. He points to a small, almost invisible detail on the schematic – a ventilation shaft leading directly into the vault.]

SCENE 2 — THE GHOST'S SIGNATURE

INT. HIDDEN SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT

LEILA

(Confused)

What is that? A ventilation shaft? It's too small for a person.

GABRIEL

Not for everyone.

He taps a key, and a small, grainy video plays on the screen. It shows a figure, impossibly thin and agile, navigating a similar shaft with ease. The figure is wearing a distinctive, almost ethereal, white mask.

LEILA

(Realizing)

The Ghost. This is her work.

GABRIEL

She's the only one who can get in and out unseen.

[Leila looks from the video to Gabriel, a new understanding dawning in her eyes. The Ghost is not just a hacker; she’s an operative.]

SCENE 3 — A NEW KIND OF DEBT

INT. HIDDEN SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT

LEILA

Why would she do this for you? What does she owe you?

Gabriel turns away, his jaw tight.

GABRIEL

It's not about debt. It's about a favor. A very old one.

He pulls up a secure comms channel. A distorted voice crackles through the speakers.

GHOST (O.S.)

Varela. You're calling in the big one.

GABRIEL

I need you inside Blackwood. The vault.

GHOST (O.S.)

(A dry chuckle)

That's a suicide mission, even for me. What's in it for me? Besides the satisfaction of watching you squirm?

[Leila watches Gabriel, realizing the true cost of this plan. He's not just risking his life; he's calling in a favor that could cost someone else theirs.]

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

Gabriel glances at Leila, then back at the screen. He takes a deep breath, his decision made.

GABRIEL

Julian Thorne. He's the target. The data. Everything.

A long silence on the other end of the line.

GHOST (O.S.)

(A low, dangerous tone)

Julian Thorne, you say? That changes things. Consider it done. But you owe me. Big.

Close on Leila’s face, illuminated by the laptop screen. She leans in, tracing a path through the digital blueprint with her finger, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination.

EPISODE 19 — The Ghost's Gambit

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

CLOSE UP on Gabriel's face, illuminated by the laptop screen. His eyes are wide, a mixture of shock and grim determination. He takes a deep, ragged breath.

SCENE 1 — Julian's New Target

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT

LEILA (30s), wrapped in a thin blanket, shivers. She watches GABRIEL (30s) intently. He's hunched over a battered laptop, a burner phone pressed to his ear. The screen shows a complex web of financial transactions, all pointing to Julian Thorne.

GABRIEL

(Into phone, low)

Julian Thorne. He's the target. The data. Everything.

A long silence on the other end of the line. Gabriel's jaw tightens.

LEILA

(Whispering)

Who is it?

Gabriel holds up a hand, silencing her.

SCENE 2 — The Price of Information

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT (CONT'D)

GHOST (O.S.)

(A low, dangerous tone)

Julian Thorne, you say? That changes things. Consider it done. But you owe me. Big.

Gabriel closes his eyes for a beat, then opens them, a flicker of resignation in their depths.

GABRIEL

(Into phone)

Understood.

He snaps the phone shut, then slams the laptop lid. The sound echoes in the vast space.

LEILA

What changes things? Who is the Ghost?

Gabriel runs a hand over his face, looking utterly drained.

GABRIEL

Someone I hoped I'd never have to call again. Someone who knows Julian.

SCENE 3 — A Debt Overdue

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT (CONT'D)

Leila pushes herself up, moving closer to him. Her voice is soft, but insistent.

LEILA

Knows him how? What did you just agree to?

Gabriel finally looks at her, his gaze heavy.

GABRIEL

The Ghost has a history with Julian. A very bad one. She'll get us the intel we need, but she'll want something in return. Something dangerous.

He gestures vaguely at the laptop.

GABRIEL (CONT'D)

She wants me to retrieve something for her. From Julian's network.

Leila's eyes widen, connecting the dots.

LEILA

You mean... you're going back in? To his inner circle?

SCENE 4 — The Digital Blueprint

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT (CONT'D)

Gabriel re-opens the laptop. The screen now displays a detailed, intricate digital blueprint of a secure server farm. It's Julian's.

GABRIEL

It's the only way. The Ghost has access, but she needs someone on the ground.

Leila stares at the blueprint, a knot forming in her stomach. The lines and nodes seem to pulse with a silent threat.

LEILA

This isn't just about data, is it? It's about revenge. For both of them.

Gabriel doesn't answer, his eyes fixed on the screen, tracing a path through the digital maze.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

CLOSE UP on Leila’s face, illuminated by the laptop screen. She leans in, tracing a path through the digital blueprint with her finger, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination. She knows this is a point of no return.

EPISODE 20 — The Ghost in the Machine

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

CLOSE UP on a flickering screen, displaying complex network schematics. A single, glowing red node pulses ominously, labeled "ARMANDATA."

SCENE 1 — Gabriel's Digital Maze

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT

LEILA stands beside GABRIEL, who is hunched over a laptop, his face illuminated by the screen's glow. The room is cold, industrial.

LEILA

(Whispering)

What is it?

Gabriel points to the pulsing node on the screen.

GABRIEL

Julian's network. It's more sophisticated than I thought. Layered.

Leila leans closer, her brow furrowed.

LEILA

And "ARMANDATA"? My family's servers?

GABRIEL

(Nods, grim)

He's not just stealing. He's weaponizing.

SCENE 2 — A Familiar Signature

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT

Leila stares at the screen, a sudden realization dawning.

LEILA

Wait. That encryption protocol... I've seen it before.

Gabriel looks at her sharply.

GABRIEL

Where?

LEILA

My father's private server. It was a bespoke system, designed by a consultant he trusted implicitly. A man named Silas.

Gabriel's fingers fly across the keyboard, cross-referencing the information.

GABRIEL

Silas... a ghost in the machine. Known for building impenetrable digital fortresses. And for disappearing when the job's done.

SCENE 3 — The Unseen Hand

INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT

Leila's mind races, connecting the dots.

LEILA

So Julian didn't just build this. He bought the architect.

GABRIEL

Or coerced him. Silas isn't known for loyalty, but he is known for self-preservation.

Leila shivers, a new layer of betrayal revealing itself.

LEILA

My father must have given Julian access. Or Silas sold him out.

Gabriel pulls up an old, grainy photo of a stern-faced man with piercing eyes.

GABRIEL

This is Silas. If we can find him, we can unravel this.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

CLOSE UP on Leila’s face, illuminated by the laptop screen. She leans in, tracing a path through the digital blueprint with her finger, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination. She knows this is a point of no return.

EPISODE 21 — The Serpent's Nest

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

[CLOSE UP on a grainy photograph of a stern-faced man with piercing eyes. The name "Silas" is scrawled beneath it. The image flickers on a laptop screen, reflected in Leila's intense gaze.]

SCENE 1 — THE DIGITAL TRAIL

[INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT]

Leila leans over Gabriel's laptop, her finger tracing a complex network diagram on the screen. Gabriel watches her, a silent sentinel.

LEILA

My father must have given Julian access. Or Silas sold him out.

GABRIEL

(Quietly)

This is Silas. If we can find him, we can unravel this.

[Leila nods, her jaw set. She clicks a few times, bringing up a map with several glowing nodes.]

LEILA

These are the known safe houses for Julian's inner circle. One of them has to be where Silas is hiding.

SCENE 2 — THE GHOST IN THE MACHINE

[INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT]

Gabriel types rapidly on the keyboard, his fingers flying. Leila watches over his shoulder.

GABRIEL

I'm cross-referencing recent financial transactions with known aliases. Silas is meticulous, but not perfect.

LEILA

He's a ghost. My father trusted him implicitly. He handled everything off-book.

[A small, red dot blinks on the map, distinct from the other nodes.]

GABRIEL

Got him. A small, untraceable transfer to a shell corporation. It’s a remote cabin, deep in the mountains.

SCENE 3 — A FAMILIAR FACE

[INT. ABANDONED WAREHOUSE - NIGHT]

Leila stares at the screen, a flicker of recognition in her eyes.

LEILA

That cabin... I know it. My father used to take me there when I was a child. It's almost impossible to get to.

GABRIEL

(Grimly)

That's why he chose it. No digital footprint, no easy access.

[Gabriel begins packing a small, tactical bag. Leila looks at him, then back at the screen.]

LEILA

He knows the Arman network inside and out. He knows our weaknesses.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

[CLOSE UP on Leila’s face, illuminated by the laptop screen. She leans in, tracing a path through the digital blueprint with her finger, her expression a mixture of terror and grim determination. She knows this is a point of no return.]

EPISODE 22 — The Unseen Hand

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

[CLOSE UP on a flickering monitor screen showing the digital blueprint of the Arman network. A cursor hovers over a deeply embedded, almost invisible file. The file opens, revealing a single, cryptic symbol: a stylized viper.]

SCENE 1 — THE VIPER'S MARK

[INT. RUSTIC SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[Leila stares at the screen, her finger tracing the viper symbol. Gabriel stands beside her, his expression grim.]

LEILA

(whispering)

The viper. It's the mark of the Black Serpent Syndicate. My grandfather spoke of them in hushed tones. A myth, he said.

GABRIEL

(low, steady)

No myth. They're real. And they're the only ones with the resources and the motive to pull off something this complex, without leaving a trace.

[Leila looks at him, a new kind of fear in her eyes.]

LEILA

Julian... he's working with them?

GABRIEL

Or for them. Either way, he's a pawn in a much bigger game.

[Gabriel gestures to the screen. The viper symbol pulses faintly.]

GABRIEL

This isn't just about money, Leila. This is about control.

SCENE 2 — THE GHOST IN THE MACHINE

[INT. RUSTIC SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[Leila types furiously on the keyboard, trying to access the embedded file. Her fingers fly, but the system remains locked.]

LEILA

It's encrypted beyond anything I've seen. Even my family's old firewalls wouldn't stand a chance.

GABRIEL

(over her shoulder)

Because it wasn't designed to be broken by a firewall. It was designed to be invisible.

[Gabriel pulls out a worn, old-school flip phone. He punches in a number, then holds it to his ear. A moment of static, then a low, distorted voice answers.]

GABRIEL (CONT'D)

Ghost? I need a deep dive. System is called 'Viper'. Arman network.

[Leila watches, mesmerized. The voice on the other end is barely audible, a series of clicks and whistles.]

LEILA

Who is that?

GABRIEL

(to phone)

No, I don't have a specific file. I have a symbol. A viper. It's a signature.

[Gabriel hangs up. He looks at Leila.]

GABRIEL (CONT'D)

One of my old contacts. A digital phantom. If anyone can find a backdoor, it's her.

SCENE 3 — THE COST OF KNOWLEDGE

[INT. RUSTIC SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[Leila paces, the implications of the Black Serpent Syndicate weighing heavily on her. Gabriel watches her.]

LEILA

My grandfather always said they were ruthless. They never left loose ends. If Julian is involved...

GABRIEL

Then he's either incredibly powerful, or incredibly stupid.

[A notification pings on Gabriel's burner phone. He glances at it, his jaw tightening.]

GABRIEL (CONT'D)

Ghost found something. But it comes with a price.

LEILA

What kind of price?

GABRIEL

She needs me to retrieve something from a secure server in Zurich. Something that will put me on the radar of a very dangerous group.

[Leila looks at him, then back at the screen with the viper symbol. The danger feels palpable.]

LEILA

You can't go. It's too risky.

GABRIEL

(his gaze unwavering)

We need to know what Julian is hiding. This is the only way.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

[CLOSE UP on Gabriel's face as he makes the call, his expression a mixture of grim determination and the heavy weight of the decision. The screen behind him still shows the pulsing viper symbol, a silent, deadly promise of what's to come.]

EPISODE 23 — The Viper's Embrace

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

[CLOSE UP on Gabriel's hand, holding a burner phone. The screen displays a pulsing, stylized viper symbol. His thumb hovers over the call button.]

SCENE 1 — A DANGEROUS DIAL

[INT. SECLUDED SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[LEILA watches GABRIEL, her face etched with a mix of fear and desperate hope. The viper symbol on the phone glows ominously.]

LEILA

(whispering)

You can't go. It's too risky.

GABRIEL

(his gaze unwavering from the phone)

We need to know what Julian is hiding. This is the only way.

[Gabriel takes a deep breath, steeling himself. He presses the call button. The line rings once, twice, then connects with a faint CLICK.]

SCENE 2 — THE COLD VOICE

[INT. SECLUDED SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[Gabriel holds the phone to his ear. Leila strains to listen, her heart pounding.]

GABRIEL

(low, controlled voice)

I understand you have something for me.

[A COLD, DISTORTED VOICE, heavily modulated, replies from the phone. It's impossible to tell if it's male or female.]

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

(calm, unsettling)

Gabriel Varela. It's been a long time. Your reputation precedes you.

[Gabriel's jaw tightens. Leila sees a flicker of something in his eyes – recognition, perhaps, or a memory he'd rather forget.]

GABRIEL

Let's keep this professional. The information.

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

Patience. All in good time. You seek the truth about Julian Thorne. A dangerous path, even for you.

SCENE 3 — A PRICE FOR TRUTH

[INT. SECLUDED SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[The Cold Voice continues, its tone chillingly amused.]

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

The information you desire comes at a price. A favor, to be exact.

GABRIEL

(tense)

What kind of favor?

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

A simple retrieval. A package. From a secure location. Nothing you haven't handled before.

[Gabriel hesitates, weighing the risks. He glances at Leila, who is now openly staring at him, silently pleading with her eyes.]

LEILA

(mouthing)

Don't.

GABRIEL

(back to the phone)

Location. Details.

SCENE 4 — THE UNEXPECTED COMPLICATION

[INT. SECLUDED SAFE HOUSE - NIGHT]

[The Cold Voice chuckles, a dry, rasping sound.]

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

Excellent. I knew you'd see reason. The package is located in a private vault, underneath the old Arman family bank.

[Leila's eyes widen in shock. The Arman family bank? Her family's legacy.]

LEILA

(whispering, horrified)

No...

COLD VOICE (O.S.)

(ignoring Leila's gasp)

You'll find the schematics encrypted on a secure server. Access code will be sent to your burner. And one more thing, Gabriel. This "package"... it's not what you expect.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

[CLOSE UP on Gabriel's face as he makes the call, his expression a mixture of grim determination and the heavy weight of the decision. The screen behind him still shows the pulsing viper symbol, a silent, deadly promise of what's to come. The phone clicks off. Gabriel slowly lowers it, his gaze meeting Leila's. Her face is pale, a dawning horror in her eyes as the implications of the Arman family bank sink in.]

EPISODE 24 — The Viper's Embrace

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)

[CLOSE UP on a small, ornate vial, filled with a shimmering, dark liquid. A single, stylized viper head is etched into the glass. A gloved hand carefully places it into a velvet-lined box.]

SCENE 1 — THE ARMORY'S SECRET

[INT. GABRIEL'S SAFE HOUSE - ARMORY - NIGHT]

The small armory is dimly lit, the metallic glint of weapons reflecting the low light. GABRIEL (30s, intense, focused) meticulously cleans a high-powered rifle. LEILA (20s, observant, wary) stands a respectful distance away, watching him.

LEILA

(Quietly)

You've been... busy.

Gabriel doesn't look up, his movements precise.

GABRIEL

Preparation. We're moving.

LEILA

(A beat)

Where?

Gabriel finally looks at her, his eyes unreadable.

GABRIEL

To a place where Julian's reach is... limited.

[Leila shivers slightly, despite herself. The thought of Julian's reach still terrifies her.]

SCENE 2 — THE VIPER'S SYMBOL

[INT. GABRIEL'S SAFE HOUSE - LIVING AREA - NIGHT]

Leila sits on a worn sofa, a tablet in her hands. She's scrolling through old news articles about the Arman family's business dealings. She stops at an article detailing a hostile takeover Julian's company attempted years ago. A small, almost hidden symbol in the corner of a corporate logo catches her eye: a stylized viper.

LEILA

(To herself)

The viper...

Gabriel enters, carrying two mugs of tea. He sets one down beside her.

GABRIEL

Find something?

Leila turns the tablet to him, pointing to the symbol.

LEILA

This. I've seen it before. On one of Julian's old business cards. And... on the side of that black van, the night I was taken.

Gabriel leans closer, his expression hardening as he studies the image.

GABRIEL

That's the mark of the 'Viper Syndicate'. A shadow organization. They specialize in corporate espionage, hostile takeovers... and 'asset removal'.

LEILA

(Voice trembling)

Asset removal? You mean... killing people?

Gabriel's silence is her answer.

SCENE 3 — THE UNEXPECTED PACKAGE

[INT. GABRIEL'S SAFE HOUSE - KITCHEN - NIGHT]

Gabriel is packing a small bag with essentials. His burner phone buzzes. He answers, his voice low.

GABRIEL (O.S.)

Varela.

A gruff, distorted voice comes through the phone.

DISTORTED VOICE (O.S.)

Package delivered. As requested.

Gabriel's eyes flick to Leila, who is now standing in the doorway, having heard the exchange.

GABRIEL

(Into phone)

Confirmed. Payment sent.

He hangs up, his jaw tight.

LEILA

(Suspiciously)

What package?

Gabriel hesitates, then walks over to a small, unmarked box on the counter. He opens it, revealing the ornate vial with the viper etching from the cold open.

GABRIEL

This.

Leila stares at the vial, her eyes wide with a mixture of fear and dawning comprehension.

LEILA

(Whispering)

What is that?

GABRIEL

(Grimly)

A very potent, untraceable sedative. Enough to incapacitate a small army.

CLIFFHANGER / EPISODE END

[CLOSE UP on the vial, the viper symbol seeming to pulse malevolently. Leila's reflection is distorted in the glass, her face pale with horror. Gabriel's hand reaches out, closing the box. He looks at Leila, his gaze unwavering, but a flicker of something akin to regret crosses his face. He knows what she's thinking. He knows what this implies. The final image is the closed box, the viper symbol the last thing we see, leaving Leila to wonder if Gabriel is preparing to protect her, or to make her disappear himself.]

EPISODE 25 — The Serpent's Coil

Duration target: 120–180 seconds

COLD OPEN (0:00–0:15)
